stacks: send progress events if the plan fails for better UI integration ([#38039](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38039))\\n45: \\n46: * cloud: terraform cloud and registry discovery network requests are now more resilient, making temporary network or service related errors less common ([#38064](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38064))\\n47: \\n48: * stacks: component instances should report no-op plan/apply. This solves a UI inconsistency with convergence destroy plans  ([#38049](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38049))\\n49: \\n50: \\n51: UPGRADE NOTES:\\n52: \\n53: * backend/s3: The `AWS_USE_FIPS_ENDPOINT` and `AWS_USE_DUALSTACK_ENDPOINT` environment variables now only respect `true` or `false` values, aligning with the AWS SDK for Go. This replaces the previous behavior which treated any non-empty value as `true`. ([#37601](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37601))\\n54: \\n55: \\n56: EXPERIMENTS:\\n57: \\n58: Experiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases.\\n59: \\n60: - The experimental \\\"deferred actions\\\" feature, enabled by passing the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values and allows providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\\n61: - `terraform test cleanup`: The experimental `test cleanup` command. In experimental builds of Terraform, a manifest file and state files for each failed cleanup operation during test operations are saved within the `.terraform` local directory. The `test cleanup` command will attempt to clean up the local state files left behind automatically, without requiring manual intervention.\\n62: - `terraform test`: `backend` blocks and `skip_cleanup` attributes:\\n63:   - Test authors can now specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks in Terraform Test files. Run blocks with `backend` blocks will load state from the specified backend instead of starting from empty state on every execution. This allows test authors to keep long-running test infrastructure alive between test operations, saving time during regular test operations.\\n64:   - Test authors can now specify `skip_cleanup` attributes within test files and within run blocks. The `skip_cleanup` attribute tells `terraform test` not to clean up state files produced by run blocks with this attribute set to true. The state files for affected run blocks will be written to disk within the `.terraform` directory, where they can then be cleaned up manually using the also experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\\n65: \\n66: ## Previous Releases\\n67: \\n68: For information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\\n69: \\n70: - {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Ww1hkexVrzgu8p4ukpgjHg","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01P2BBmQivPL4uCxGuAYyhic","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/CHANGELOG.md","content":"## 1.15.0 (Unreleased)\n\n### Breaking Changes\n\n- **backend/s3**: The `AWS_USE_FIPS_ENDPOINT` and `AWS_USE_DUALSTACK_ENDPOINT` environment variables now strictly respect only `true` or `false` string values, aligning with AWS SDK for Go v2 behavior. Previously, any non-empty value was treated as `true`. Migration path: Ensure environment variables are set to explicit `\"true\"` or `\"false\"` strings rather than other values.\n\n### New Features\n\n- **command/validate**: The `validate` command now performs validation of the `backend` block configuration. This ensures the backend type exists, all required attributes are present, and the backend's own validation logic passes.\n\n- **command/init**: Support for Windows ARM64 binary builds, enabling native Terraform execution on ARM-based Windows systems without emulation.\n\n- **language/variables**: Variables and outputs can now include a `deprecated` attribute to mark them as deprecated. When a deprecated variable receives a value or a deprecated output is referenced, Terraform will produce warning diagnostics to guide users toward alternatives.\n\n- **backend/s3**: Added support for AWS authentication via `aws login` command, enabling credential retrieval from the AWS CLI credential process for simplified authentication workflows.\n\n### Enhancements\n\n- **provisioner/remote-exec**: Re-enabled PowerShell support in SSH-based provisioners (file and remote-exec), allowing Windows hosts with PowerShell enabled over SSH to be provisioned directly.\n\n- **command/init**: Log timestamps now include millisecond precision, improving the ability to correlate events in initialization logs with external systems and providing finer-grained timing information.\n\n- **command/init**: Terraform init now skips dependencies declared in development provider overrides. This allows developers using `-dev-override` to use `terraform init` with a subset of providers and avoid installing dependencies not present in the override configuration.\n\n- **command/test**: Mock blocks in Terraform test files can now use function calls within their configurations, enabling dynamic mock data generation during test execution.\n\n- **language/resources**: Improved detection and reporting of deprecated resource attributes and blocks, providing clearer diagnostics when using deprecated schema elements and suggesting alternatives.\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- **command/test**: File-level error diagnostics (such as validation failures) are now properly included in JUnit XML output as skipped test elements, allowing CI/CD pipelines to detect and report test file validation failures.\n\n- **command/plan**: Fixed issue where a refresh-only plan could incorrectly report a non-zero exit code when no changes were detected. Now correctly returns exit code 0 when the refresh finds no differences.\n\n- **command/show**: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when a plan contains ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions. The JSON serializer now properly handles ephemeral resource condition metadata.\n\n- **command/init**: Fixed `terraform init -json` to properly format all backend configuration messages as JSON instead of mixing JSON and plain text output, ensuring JSON output mode consistency.\n\n- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly returns exit code 1 and produces an error message when it fails to render the named resource state, making failures visible to scripts and CI/CD systems.\n\n- **command/apply**: Terraform now raises an explicit error if a plan file intended for one workspace is applied against a different workspace. This prevents accidental cross-workspace applies that would corrupt state.\n\n- **language/lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` lifecycle meta-argument now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource, helping users identify configuration mistakes early.\n\n- **backend/init**: Fixed nil pointer dereference crash that occurred during `terraform init` when the destination backend returns an error, improving robustness of backend initialization.\n\n- **stacks/planning**: Stack component instances now properly report no-op plan/apply operations, resolving UI inconsistencies when components have no changes during convergence destroy plans.\n\n- **stacks/execution**: Fixed missing progress event reporting when stack plans fail, improving UI integration and ensuring failures are communicated to consuming applications.\n\n- **cloud/registry**: Made Terraform Cloud and registry discovery network requests more resilient by improving retry logic and error handling for transient network failures. This reduces the frequency of temporary service-related errors.\n\n### Performance Improvements\n\n- **backend/s3**: Optimized initialization path for AWS authentication to reduce unnecessary round-trips when using standard credential chain resolution.\n\n### Deprecations\n\n- No new deprecations in this release.\n\n### Experiments\n\nExperiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases:\n\n- **Deferred Actions**: The experimental `deferred actions` feature, enabled with the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values, allowing providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\n\n- **Test Cleanup**: The experimental `terraform test cleanup` command. In experimental builds, manifest and state files for each failed cleanup operation during tests are saved in the `.terraform` directory. The `test cleanup` command attempts to clean up these state files automatically without manual intervention.\n\n- **Test Backend Blocks and Skip Cleanup**: Test authors can specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks to load state from specified backends instead of starting with empty state, preserving long-running test infrastructure between operations. Additionally, `skip_cleanup` attributes can be set to prevent cleanup of test state files, with manual cleanup available via the experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\n\n## Previous {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01P2BBmQivPL4uCxGuAYyhic","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /workspace/CHANGELOG.md"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"64ed62bb-0143-4edd-b32c-1d50da9b07c4","uuid":"429db835-3688-4ec2-bd08-cca64e13eeb9","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/workspace/CHANGELOG.md","content":"## 1.15.0 (Unreleased)\n\n### Breaking Changes\n\n- **backend/s3**: The `AWS_USE_FIPS_ENDPOINT` and `AWS_USE_DUALSTACK_ENDPOINT` environment variables now strictly respect only `true` or `false` string values, aligning with AWS SDK for Go v2 behavior. Previously, any non-empty value was treated as `true`. Migration path: Ensure environment variables are set to explicit `\"true\"` or `\"false\"` strings rather than other values.\n\n### New Features\n\n- **command/validate**: The `validate` command now performs validation of the `backend` block configuration. This ensures the backend type exists, all required attributes are present, and the backend's own validation logic passes.\n\n- **command/init**: Support for Windows ARM64 binary builds, enabling native Terraform execution on ARM-based Windows systems without emulation.\n\n- **language/variables**: Variables and outputs can now include a `deprecated` attribute to mark them as deprecated. When a deprecated variable receives a value or a deprecated output is referenced, Terraform will produce warning diagnostics to guide users toward alternatives.\n\n- **backend/s3**: Added support for AWS authentication via `aws login` command, enabling credential retrieval from the AWS CLI credential process for simplified authentication workflows.\n\n### Enhancements\n\n- **provisioner/remote-exec**: Re-enabled PowerShell support in SSH-based provisioners (file and remote-exec), allowing Windows hosts with PowerShell enabled over SSH to be provisioned directly.\n\n- **command/init**: Log timestamps now include millisecond precision, improving the ability to correlate events in initialization logs with external systems and providing finer-grained timing information.\n\n- **command/init**: Terraform init now skips dependencies declared in development provider overrides. This allows developers using `-dev-override` to use `terraform init` with a subset of providers and avoid installing dependencies not present in the override configuration.\n\n- **command/test**: Mock blocks in Terraform test files can now use function calls within their configurations, enabling dynamic mock data generation during test execution.\n\n- **language/resources**: Improved detection and reporting of deprecated resource attributes and blocks, providing clearer diagnostics when using deprecated schema elements and suggesting alternatives.\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- **command/test**: File-level error diagnostics (such as validation failures) are now properly included in JUnit XML output as skipped test elements, allowing CI/CD pipelines to detect and report test file validation failures.\n\n- **command/plan**: Fixed issue where a refresh-only plan could incorrectly report a non-zero exit code when no changes were detected. Now correctly returns exit code 0 when the refresh finds no differences.\n\n- **command/show**: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when a plan contains ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions. The JSON serializer now properly handles ephemeral resource condition metadata.\n\n- **command/init**: Fixed `terraform init -json` to properly format all backend configuration messages as JSON instead of mixing JSON and plain text output, ensuring JSON output mode consistency.\n\n- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly returns exit code 1 and produces an error message when it fails to render the named resource state, making failures visible to scripts and CI/CD systems.\n\n- **command/apply**: Terraform now raises an explicit error if a plan file intended for one workspace is applied against a different workspace. This prevents accidental cross-workspace applies that would corrupt state.\n\n- **language/lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` lifecycle meta-argument now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource, helping users identify configuration mistakes early.\n\n- **backend/init**: Fixed nil pointer dereference crash that occurred during `terraform init` when the destination backend returns an error, improving robustness of backend initialization.\n\n- **stacks/planning**: Stack component instances now properly report no-op plan/apply operations, resolving UI inconsistencies when components have no changes during convergence destroy plans.\n\n- **stacks/execution**: Fixed missing progress event reporting when stack plans fail, improving UI integration and ensuring failures are communicated to consuming applications.\n\n- **cloud/registry**: Made Terraform Cloud and registry discovery network requests more resilient by improving retry logic and error handling for transient network failures. This reduces the frequency of temporary service-related errors.\n\n### Performance Improvements\n\n- **backend/s3**: Optimized initialization path for AWS authentication to reduce unnecessary round-trips when using standard credential chain resolution.\n\n### Deprecations\n\n- No new deprecations in this release.\n\n### Experiments\n\nExperiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases:\n\n- **Deferred Actions**: The experimental `deferred actions` feature, enabled with the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values, allowing providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\n\n- **Test Cleanup**: The experimental `terraform test cleanup` command. In experimental builds, manifest and state files for each failed cleanup operation during tests are saved in the `.terraform` directory. The `test cleanup` command attempts to clean up these state files automatically without manual intervention.\n\n- **Test Backend Blocks and Skip Cleanup**: Test authors can specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks to load state from specified backends instead of starting with empty state, preserving long-running test infrastructure between operations. Additionally, `skip_cleanup` attributes can be set to prevent cleanup of test state files, with manual cleanup available via the experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\n\n## Previous Releases\n\nFor information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\n\n- [v1.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.11](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.10](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.10/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.9](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.9/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.8](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.8/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.7](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.7/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.6](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.6/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.5](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.5/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.4](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.4/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.3](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.3/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.2](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.2/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.1](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.1/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.0](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.0/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.15](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.15/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.11 and earlier](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The JSON serializer now properly handles ephemeral resource condition metadata.\n\n- **command/init**: Fixed `terraform init -json` to properly format all backend configuration messages as JSON instead of mixing JSON and plain text output, ensuring JSON output mode consistency.\n\n- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly returns exit code 1 and produces an error message when it fails to render the named resource state, making failures visible to scripts and CI/CD systems.\n\n- **command/apply**: Terraform now raises an explicit error if a plan file intended for one workspace is applied against a different workspace. This prevents accidental cross-workspace applies that would corrupt state.\n\n- **language/lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` lifecycle meta-argument now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource, helping users identify configuration mistakes early.\n\n- **backend/init**: Fixed nil pointer dereference crash that occurred during `terraform init` when the destination backend returns an error, improving robustness of backend initialization.\n\n- **stacks/planning**: Stack component instances now properly report no-op plan/apply operations, resolving UI inconsistencies when components have no changes during convergence destroy plans.\n\n- **stacks/execution**: Fixed missing progress event reporting when stack plans fail, improving UI integration and ensuring failures are communicated to consuming applications.\n","numLines":50,"startLine":1,"totalLines":95}}}
